# StaffOrdersMobile Bug Tracker

**Page:** `pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx`
**Last updated:** 2026-04-06 (Chain c05c â€” SOM Section Rework: lifecycle order, active/passive, dual metric, 2-step requests, staff pill, inline toast, close-blocker, bulk requests)

---

## Fixed Bugs

### SOM-KS1-P0-01 (P0) -- activeRequests filter excludes 'accepted' status
- **Function:** activeRequests useMemo filter (line ~3310)
- **Root cause:** Filter only included `["new", "in_progress"]` â€” accepted requests vanished from UI, making two-step flow impossible.
- **Fix:** Changed to `!["done", "cancelled"].includes(r.status)` â€” now includes accepted requests.
- **Chain:** staffordersmobile-260406-195641-c05c
- **Status:** ðŸŸ¡ Fixed (pending test)

### SOM-KS1-P0-02 (P0) -- updateRequestMutation only passes status, loses assignee
- **Function:** updateRequestMutation mutationFn (line ~3315)
- **Root cause:** Destructured only `{id, status}` â€” Accept step needed `assignee` + `assigned_at` fields.
- **Fix:** Changed to spread all payload fields to update call.
- **Chain:** staffordersmobile-260406-195641-c05c
- **Status:** ðŸŸ¡ Fixed (pending test)

### SOM-KS1-P0-03 (P0) -- onCloseRequest hardcodes 'done', ignores status parameter
- **Function:** onCloseRequest prop (line ~4190)
- **Root cause:** Status param from child was ignored â€” always sent 'done'. Accept button would incorrectly close request instead of accepting.
- **Fix:** Changed to pass `newStatus` and `extraFields` from child component.
- **Chain:** staffordersmobile-260406-195641-c05c
- **Status:** ðŸŸ¡ Fixed (pending test)

### SOM-KS1-01 (P1) -- Sections in wrong lifecycle order (Ready before InProgress)
- **Root cause:** Ready rendered before InProgress in all 3+1 blocks. Lifecycle should be: New â†’ InProgress â†’ Ready â†’ Served.
- **Fix:** Swapped InProgress before Ready in compact, expanded, compact-table, and legacy blocks.
- **Chain:** staffordersmobile-260406-195641-c05c
- **Status:** ðŸŸ¡ Fixed (pending test)

### SOM-KS1-02 (P1) -- No visual distinction between active/passive sections
- **Fix:** Active headers (Requests, New, Ready) get bg pill; passive (InProgress, Served) get opacity-60.
- **Chain:** staffordersmobile-260406-195641-c05c
- **Status:** ðŸŸ¡ Fixed (pending test)

### SOM-KS1-03 (P1) -- Section headers show single count, need dual metric
- **Fix:** Added `pluralRu` helper. Headers now show "N Ð³Ð¾ÑÑ‚ÑŒ Â· M Ð±Ð»ÑŽÐ´" format in all blocks.
- **Chain:** staffordersmobile-260406-195641-c05c
- **Status:** ðŸŸ¡ Fixed (pending test)

### SOM-KS1-04 (P1) -- Request buttons: single "Ð’Ñ‹Ð¿Ð¾Ð»Ð½ÐµÐ½Ð¾" instead of two-step flow
- **Fix:** Conditional render: new requests â†’ blue "ÐŸÑ€Ð¸Ð½ÑÑ‚ÑŒ" (sets accepted + assignee), accepted â†’ green "Ð’Ñ‹Ð´Ð°Ñ‚ÑŒ" (sets done) + staff pill. All 3 render blocks updated.

- **Status:** ðŸŸ¡ Fixed (pending test)

### SOM-KS1-05 (P1) -- Close-table shows only first blocker, not all

### SOM-KS1-06 (P1) -- No bulk request buttons

### SOM-KS1-07 (P1) -- Undo toast: global fixed position instead of inline

### SOM-S213-01 (P1) -- Batch "Ð’Ñ‹Ð´Ð°Ñ‚ÑŒ Ð²ÑÑ‘" button does not trigger undo toast
- **Function:** OrderGroupCard, Section 2 batch button onClick handler
- **Root cause:** The batch "Ð’Ñ‹Ð´Ð°Ñ‚ÑŒ Ð²ÑÑ‘" button called `handleBatchAction(completedOrders)` directly without building snapshots or calling `setUndoToast`. Individual per-order buttons had the correct undo pattern, but the batch button was missing it.
- **Fix:** Replaced onClick handler to build snapshots array from completedOrders, call handleBatchAction, then call setUndoToast with snapshots/timerId/onUndo callback (same pattern as individual order buttons ~line 1951-1965).
- **Chain:** staffordersmobile-260401-114201-9ed3
- **Status:** ðŸŸ¡ Fixed (pending test)

### SOM-UX-24 (P2) -- No "Ð’Ð«Ð”ÐÐÐž" section for served orders
- **Function:** OrderGroupCard, new Section 4
- **Root cause:** Once orders reach `served` status, they are excluded from `activeOrders` filter. The table card disappears entirely when all orders are served. No way for waiter to see what was already delivered.
- **Fix:** Added `servedExpanded` state, `servedOrders` useQuery (lazy, enabled when expanded + table type), and collapsed-by-default Ð’Ð«Ð”ÐÐÐž section with slate-400 muted styling, 44px touch target header, toggle show/hide, read-only rows with guestName + time.
- **Chain:** staffordersmobile-260401-114201-9ed3
- **Status:** ðŸŸ¡ Fixed (pending test)

### SOM-UX-23 (P1) -- Collapsed card Row 3: replace Ð¡Ð•Ð™Ð§ÐÐ¡/Ð•Ð©Ð with per-stage lines
- **Function:** TableCard collapsed view, Row 3
- **Root cause:** Old Row 3 showed hardcoded Â«Ð¡Ð•Ð™Ð§ÐÐ¡/Ð•Ð©ÐÂ» labels with static stage names and total sum â€” noise for waiter, no urgency info
- **Fix:** Added `summaryLines` useMemo grouping activeOrders by stage via `getStatusConfig`, with per-line age from `stage_entered_at || created_date`. Color coding: red >15min / amber 5-15min / neutral <5min (requests: red â‰¥3min). Forward-compatible `show_in_summary` filter for #218.
- **Chain:** staffordersmobile-260331-225506-fac7
- **Status:** âœ… TESTED S212 (collapsed card shows per-stage lines with urgency color)

### BUG-S66-01 (P1) -- Detail view doesn't open on card tap (Sprint B broken)
- **Function:** TableDetailScreen render / CSS animation
- **Root cause:** CSS `translate-x-full` â†’ `translate-x-0` transition with `requestAnimationFrame` timing was unreliable in Base44 platform container. Detail screen mounted but stayed off-screen.
- **Fix:** Removed slide-in animation entirely. Detail view now shows instantly with `z-50` (above all other content). Swipe-right to close gesture retained.
- **Commit:** `9b27dfd`
- **RELEASE:** `260302-05 StaffOrdersMobile RELEASE.jsx`
- **Status:** FIXED

### BUG-S66-02 (P1) -- No CTA button on PREPARING card
- **Function:** computeGroupCTA
- **Root cause:** `computeGroupCTA` returned `null` for all PREPARING status cards (by Sprint A design V2-06). Orders in middle stages (kitchen working) had no action button, preventing waiter from advancing them.
- **Fix:** For PREPARING status, find orders with `nextStageId`/`nextStatus` that are advanceable (not first-stage, not finish-stage). Show CTA with appropriate action label. Added `ctaBgClass` for PREPARING style.
- **Commit:** `aba6513`
- **RELEASE:** `260302-05 StaffOrdersMobile RELEASE.jsx`
- **Status:** FIXED

### BUG-S65-04 (P1) -- Waiter accepts order blind (no content visible)
- **Function:** computeGroupCTA / handleCTA
- **Root cause:** CTA on collapsed card for NEW orders directly advanced the order status (accepting it) without showing the order content (dishes, quantities). Waiter had no idea what they were accepting.
- **Fix:** First-stage CTA now opens the detail view (calls `onCardBodyTap`) instead of advancing directly. Label changed from "ÐŸÑ€Ð¸Ð½ÑÑ‚ÑŒ" to "ÐžÑ‚ÐºÑ€Ñ‹Ñ‚ÑŒ Ð·Ð°ÐºÐ°Ð·". Accept button remains in the detail view (GuestOrderSection) where order content is visible.
- **Commit:** `4f2fa26`
- **RELEASE:** `260302-05 StaffOrdersMobile RELEASE.jsx`
- **Status:** FIXED

### BUG-S65-05 (P2) -- Double "Ð¡Ñ‚Ð¾Ð»" prefix ("Ð¡Ñ‚Ð¾Ð» Ð¡Ñ‚Ð¾Ð» 22")
- **Function:** orderGroups computation / banner text
- **Root cause:** `displayName` was constructed as `` `Ð¡Ñ‚Ð¾Ð» ${tableName}` `` where `tableName` comes from `tableMap[tableId].name` which already contains "Ð¡Ñ‚Ð¾Ð»" prefix (DB stores "Ð¡Ñ‚Ð¾Ð» 22"). Same issue in banner notification text.
- **Fix:** Removed hardcoded "Ð¡Ñ‚Ð¾Ð» " prefix from `displayName` in orderGroups computation and from single-table banner text. Table name used as-is from DB.
- **Commit:** `5200dc7`
- **RELEASE:** `260302-05 StaffOrdersMobile RELEASE.jsx`
- **Status:** FIXED

### BUG-SM-011 (P0) -- Hall orders without table_session shown in active view
- **Function:** activeOrders (useMemo filter)
- **Root cause:** Hall orders with `table_session: null` (legacy/orphan data from before session logic was implemented, or orders created when session expired) passed through the filter and appeared in the waiter's active orders list. Combined with BUG-PM-009 (sessions never expired), this caused historical orders to appear mixed with current ones.
- **Fix:** Added filter: `if (o.order_type === 'hall' && !getLinkId(o.table_session)) return false` in `activeOrders` computation. Hall orders without a valid `table_session` link are now excluded from the active view.
- **Commit:** `9dae0cc`
- **RELEASE:** `260302-04 StaffOrdersMobile RELEASE.jsx`
- **Status:** FIXED

- **Fix:** Added error toast for non-rate-limit failures

### BUG-SM-014 (P0) -- Detail view shows stale orders (new orders not visible)
- **Function:** handleOpenDetail / notification effect / computeTableStatus
- **Root cause:** Detail view relied solely on polling for updates. When opened, it showed cached data without forcing a fresh fetch. Additionally, computeTableStatus checked STALE before NEW, so tables with new first-stage orders could show "ÐŸÐ ÐžÐ¡Ð ÐžÐ§Ð•Ð" instead of "ÐÐžÐ’Ð«Ð™".
- **Fix:** (1) `handleOpenDetail` now calls `refetchOrders()` on open. (2) Notification effect invalidates orders query when new orders detected. (3) Reordered `computeTableStatus` â€” NEW check before STALE, so new orders clear ÐŸÐ ÐžÐ¡Ð ÐžÐ§Ð•Ð. (4) Detail view closes after table close to prevent zombie view.
- **RELEASE:** `260304-00 StaffOrdersMobile RELEASE.jsx`
- **Status:** FIXED

### BUG-SM-007 (P0 â€” upgraded from P2) -- Close table without confirmation dialog
- **Function:** handleCloseTable
- **Root cause:** Used browser `confirm()` â€” ugly, not mobile-friendly, easy to accidentally confirm. Single tap closes table, guests lose ability to order.
- **Fix:** Replaced with React state-driven confirmation dialog: title with table name ("Ð—Ð°ÐºÑ€Ñ‹Ñ‚ÑŒ Ð¡Ñ‚Ð¾Ð» 5?"), descriptive text, destructive red button, 44px touch targets, mobile 320px safe. Callers now pass table name as second argument.
- **RELEASE:** `260304-00 StaffOrdersMobile RELEASE.jsx`
- **Status:** FIXED

### BUG-SM-012 (P0) -- No scheduled session cleanup (SESS-016)
- **Function:** (missing â€” no cleanup job existed)
- **Root cause:** Base44 has no built-in scheduler. Expired sessions (>8h) with no problem orders stayed `open` forever, causing stale data accumulation and historical orders appearing to new guests.
- **Fix:** Created `components/sessionCleanupJob.js` â€” `runSessionCleanup()` function that: (1) queries all open sessions, (2) checks 8h hard-expire via `isSessionExpired()`, (3) skips sessions with problem orders (non-finish or unpaid), (4) expires safe sessions. Includes `dryRun` mode for testing.
- **Integration:** Wired into StaffOrdersMobile via `useEffect + setInterval(5min)` â€” runs on mount then every 300s.
- **RELEASE:** `260303-02 sessionCleanupJob RELEASE.js` + `260303-06 StaffOrdersMobile RELEASE.jsx`
- **Commit:** `c30f1a9` (P1 fix) + `f2d6f41` (integration)
- **Status:** FIXED

### BUG-SM-013 (P1) -- payment_status always undefined for hall orders
- **Function:** isProblemOrder in sessionCleanupJob.js
- **Root cause:** Hall orders are created without `payment_status` field (undefined), while pickup/delivery orders set it to `"unpaid"`. The check `order.payment_status === 'unpaid'` missed undefined values, treating hall orders as "paid" â€” a false negative that would wrongly allow sessions to close when payment tracking is enabled.
- **Fix:** Changed check from `=== 'unpaid'` to `!== 'paid'`. Now undefined/null/unpaid all correctly flag as problem orders.
- **RELEASE:** `260303-02 sessionCleanupJob RELEASE.js`
- **Commit:** `c30f1a9`
- **Status:** FIXED

### BUG-SO-S61-07 (P2) -- "Ð¡Ñ‚Ð¾Ð» Ð¡Ñ‚Ð¾Ð» 1" double prefix REGRESSION
- **Function:** RequestCard / OrderCard / table picker / orderGroups
- **Root cause:** 5 locations added hardcoded `"Ð¡Ñ‚Ð¾Ð» "` prefix to table names that already contain the prefix from DB. Previous fix in v2.7.2 only addressed the group header.
- **Fix:** Added `withTablePrefix()` helper that checks `name.startsWith("Ð¡Ñ‚Ð¾Ð» ")` before adding prefix. Applied to all 5 locations: RequestCard (line 714), OrderCard (line 883, 892), table picker (line 1283), orderGroups (line 2404).
- **Commit:** `ece5c64`
- **RELEASE:** `260306-01 StaffOrdersMobile RELEASE.jsx`
- **Status:** FIXED

### BUG-SO-S89-01 (P1) -- Raw i18n key `orderprocess.default.new` in status badge â€” REGRESSION
- **Function:** getStatusConfig / getStageName
- **Root cause:** OrderStage entity stores i18n keys (like `orderprocess.default.new`) in the `name` field instead of display names. `getStatusConfig` returned `stage.name` directly as label, showing raw keys.
- **Fix v1 (S89-S90):** Added `STAGE_NAME_FALLBACKS` map + `getStageName()` helper. Deployed as 260306-04 but bug persisted.
- **Fix v2 (S91):** Made `getStageName` more robust: (1) tries `t()` first for proper B44 i18n, (2) added short name mappings ("new" â†’ "ÐÐ¾Ð²Ñ‹Ð¹"), (3) added dotted-key last-segment extraction, (4) added fallback protection to STATUS_FLOW path too.
- **Commit:** `a3727f4` (v1 S89), `03bab9e` (v1 restored S90), `8be58c6` (v2 S91)
- **RELEASE:** `260306-05 StaffOrdersMobile RELEASE.jsx`
- **Status:** FIXED (v2)

### PM-158 (P1) -- Order statuses don't update in CartView after StaffOrdersMobile status change
- **Function:** handleAction, handleAdvance, getStatusConfig
- **Root cause:** When OrderStages are configured, `handleAction` and `handleAdvance` update only `stage_id` in DB payload, never `status`. CartView polls `order.status` for bucket sorting â†’ orders stay in "ÐÐ¾Ð²Ñ‹Ð¹ Ð·Ð°ÐºÐ°Ð·" bucket forever.
- **Fix:** (1) Added `nextStageInternalCode` to `getStatusConfig` stage-mode return object. (2) In `handleAction` and `handleAdvance`, added CODE_TO_STATUS mapping to derive and set `payload.status` alongside `stage_id` when internal_code is recognized.
- **Commit:** `b91919d`
- **Chain:** staffordersmobile-260329-155109-3e10
- **Status:** FIXED

278:function getStageName(stage, t) {
279:  if (!stage?.name) return "—";
280:  const name = stage.name;
281:  // 1. Try t() if available (proper B44 i18n)
282:  if (t) {
283:    const translated = t(name);
284:    if (translated && translated !== name) return translated;
285:  }
286:  // 2. Direct lookup in fallback map (exact key or short name)
287:  if (STAGE_NAME_FALLBACKS[name]) return STAGE_NAME_FALLBACKS[name];
288:  // 3. Extract last segment from dotted key (e.g. "orderprocess.foo.new" → "new")
289:  if (name.includes('.')) {
290:    const lastSegment = name.split('.').pop();
291:    if (STAGE_NAME_FALLBACKS[lastSegment]) return STAGE_NAME_FALLBACKS[lastSegment];
292:  }
293:  // 4. Return raw name as last resort
294:  return name;
295:}

359:function formatCompactMinutes(totalMinutes) {
360:  if (!Number.isFinite(totalMinutes) || totalMinutes <= 0) return "0\u043C";
361:  if (totalMinutes < 60) return `${totalMinutes}\u043C`;
362:  const hours = Math.floor(totalMinutes / 60);
363:  const minutes = totalMinutes % 60;
364:  return minutes > 0 ? `${hours}\u0447 ${minutes}\u043C` : `${hours}\u0447`;
365:}

367:function formatHallMoney(amount) {
368:  const value = Number(amount || 0);
369:  const hasFraction = Math.abs(value % 1) > 0;
370:  return `${value.toLocaleString("ru-RU", {
371:    minimumFractionDigits: hasFraction ? 2 : 0,
372:    maximumFractionDigits: 2,
373:  })} \u20B8`;
374:}

911:    }

913:  
914:  // Fallback: start of today
915:  const startOfToday = new Date(now);
916:  startOfToday.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
917:  return startOfToday;
918:}

1038:function createBeep() {
1039:  try {
1040:    const AudioCtx = window.AudioContext || window.webkitAudioContext;
1041:    if (!AudioCtx) return null;
1042:    const ctx = new AudioCtx();
1043:    return {
1044:      ctx,
1045:      play: () => {
1046:        const o = ctx.createOscillator();
1047:        const g = ctx.createGain();
1048:        o.type = "sine";
1049:        o.frequency.value = 880;
1050:        g.gain.value = 0.03;
1051:        o.connect(g);
1052:        g.connect(ctx.destination);
1053:        o.start();
1054:        o.stop(ctx.currentTime + 0.08);
1055:      },
1056:      resume: async () => {
1057:        try {
1058:          if (ctx.state === "suspended") await ctx.resume();
1059:        } catch { /* ignore */ }
1060:      },
1061:    };
1062:  } catch {
1063:    return null;
1064:  }
1065:}

I found a likely high-impact multi-tenant bug pattern: several data queries fall back to global `.list()` when `partnerId` is falsy, while at least one of those queries is enabled before `partnerId` is explicitly required. I’m validating the surrounding auth/token flow now to make sure that’s a real leak path and not just dead code.

3613:  useEffect(() => {
3614:    // Kitchen doesn't see guest badges — don't load guests
3615:    if (isKitchen) return;
3616:    
3617:    async function loadGuestsBatch() {
3618:      // Protect from undefined (orders may be undefined before loading)
3619:      const list = roleFilteredOrders || [];
3620:      
3621:      // P0-4: Use ref to filter already-attempted IDs (not just guestsMap)
3622:      const guestIds = [...new Set(
3623:        list
3624:          .map(o => getLinkId(o.guest))
3625:          .filter(Boolean)
3626:          .filter(id => !loadedGuestIdsRef.current.has(id)) // P0-4: check ref instead of guestsMap
3627:      )];
3628:      
3629:      if (guestIds.length === 0) return;
3630:      
3631:      // P0-4: Mark as attempted BEFORE loading (prevents parallel duplicate requests)
3632:      guestIds.forEach(id => loadedGuestIdsRef.current.add(id));
3633:      
3634:      try {
3635:        // Load in parallel
3636:        const guestPromises = guestIds.map(id => 
3637:          base44.entities.SessionGuest.get(id).catch(() => null)
3638:        );
3639:        const guests = await Promise.all(guestPromises);
3640:        
3641:        // Single setState
3642:        const newMap = {};
3643:        guests.forEach((guest, idx) => {
3644:          if (guest) newMap[guestIds[idx]] = guest;
3645:        });
3646:        
3647:        if (Object.keys(newMap).length > 0) {
3648:          setGuestsMap(prev => ({ ...prev, ...newMap }));
3649:        }
3650:      } catch (err) {
3651:        console.error("Error loading guests batch:", err);
3652:        // P0-4: On error, we keep IDs in ref to avoid retrying failed IDs repeatedly
3653:      }
3654:    }
3655:    
3656:    loadGuestsBatch();
3657:  }, [roleFilteredOrders, isKitchen]); // P0-4: deps are correct now (loadedGuestIdsRef is ref, doesn't need to be in deps)

+# Code Review Report: `task-260414-191537` `staffordersmobile.jsx`
+
+Reviewed file:
+- `C:\Dev\worktrees\task-260414-191537\pages\StaffOrdersMobile\staffordersmobile.jsx`
+
+Context reviewed:
+- `C:\Dev\worktrees\task-260414-191537\pages\StaffOrdersMobile\StaffOrdersMobile README.md`
+- `C:\Dev\worktrees\task-260414-191537\pages\StaffOrdersMobile\BUGS.md`
+
+Note:
+- The target worktree is outside the writable sandbox, so this report is saved in the current review repo mirror under `pages/StaffOrdersMobile/`.
+
+## Findings
+
+### [P1] Logout unbind race regressed
+- **Lines:** 3261-3273
+- **Problem:** `handleLogout()` calls `updateLinkMutation.mutate(...)`, then immediately clears local state and redirects after 500ms. If the network request has not completed, the device can remain bound to the token link. `BUGS.md` already lists this as fixed earlier, so the current file has reintroduced the race.
+- **Impact:** Staff can get locked out on the next login because the previous device binding was never reliably cleared.
+- **FIX:** Make `handleLogout` async, await `updateLinkMutation.mutateAsync()` or `base44.entities.StaffAccessLink.update(...)`, handle failure with a toast, then clear local storage and navigate only after the unbind attempt finishes.
+
+### [P1] Order status mutations fail silently and do not surface 429 state
+- **Lines:** 1594-1606, 1904-1920
+- **Problem:** `updateStatusMutation` and `advanceMutation` only roll back optimistic cache in `onError`. They do not show any error toast and do not set `rateLimitHit` on 429 responses, unlike several other mutations in the file.
+- **Impact:** Waiters tap an action, the UI snaps back or does nothing, and there is no explanation. In real service flow this looks like a broken button.
+- **FIX:** In both `onError` handlers, detect `isRateLimitError(err)` and switch into the rate-limit screen path (`cancelQueries()` + `setRateLimitHit(true)`), and show a translated error toast for all non-429 failures.
+
+### [P1] Partner scoping can fall back to global `.list()` queries
+- **Lines:** 3351-3373, 3494-3519
+- **Problem:** `tables`, `orders`, and `serviceRequests` use `.list()` when `partnerId` is falsy:
+  - `Table.list()` at 3371
+  - `Order.list("-created_date", 1000)` at 3496
+  - `ServiceRequest.list()` at 3518
+  Their `enabled` conditions do not consistently require `partnerId`.
+- **Impact:** If link/user data is incomplete or malformed, this page can fetch unscoped cross-restaurant data. In a multi-tenant Base44 app, that is a serious data-isolation bug.
+- **FIX:** Require `!!partnerId` before enabling these queries, remove the global `.list()` fallback, and show a blocking error state when partner context cannot be resolved.
+
+### [P1] i18n is still missing across the page
+- **Lines:** 220-349, 418-420, 921-924, 2914-2930, 3363, 4139-4186, 4217-4552
+- **Problem:** The page uses `useI18n()` only for stage-name translation, but most user-facing UI is still hardcoded in Russian:
+  - `STATUS_FLOW`, `TYPE_THEME`, `REQUEST_TYPE_LABELS`, `HALL_UI_TEXT`, `ROLE_LABELS`
+  - toast messages and dialog labels
+  - header labels and button text
+  - fallbacks like `"Ресторан"`, `"стол"`, `"Ссылка недействительна."`
+  - `formatRelativeTime()` is hard-wired to `date-fns/locale/ru`
+- **Impact:** This violates the project i18n rule and makes the page impossible to localize correctly. `BUGS.md` already tracks this as `BUG-SM-001`, so the issue remains unresolved.
+- **FIX:** Convert text constants into functions that accept `t`, replace all user-facing strings with `t('page.section.key')`, and derive date/number locale from the active i18n locale instead of hardcoding Russian formatting.
+
+### [P1] AudioContext cleanup regression
+- **Lines:** 1038-1065, 2959-2975
+- **Problem:** `createBeep()` allocates an `AudioContext`, and mount logic stores it in `audioRef.current`, but there is no unmount cleanup that calls `ctx.close()`. `BUGS.md` already records this as a previously fixed issue.
+- **Impact:** Re-entering this screen repeatedly can leak audio contexts on mobile browsers, eventually breaking sound notifications or hitting browser context limits.
+- **FIX:** Add a cleanup effect that calls `audioRef.current?.ctx?.close()` on unmount and then clears the ref.
+
+### [P2] Service request and bulk-close failures still have incomplete error feedback
+- **Lines:** 3550-3557, 4167-4178
+- **Problem:** `updateRequestMutation` only handles rate-limit failures; all other errors are silent. `handleCloseAllOrders()` also only handles the rate-limit branch and otherwise exits without any feedback.
+- **Impact:** Staff can tap request actions or bulk-close flows and receive no visible error when the backend rejects the operation.
+- **FIX:** Add translated error toasts for non-429 failures and surface partial batch failures with a summary toast instead of failing silently.
+
+### [P2] Guest-name caching can permanently hide names after transient request failures
+- **Lines:** 3617-3653
+- **Problem:** Guest IDs are inserted into `loadedGuestIdsRef` before loading starts. Each `SessionGuest.get(id)` failure is swallowed with `.catch(() => null)`, so failed IDs remain marked as attempted and are never retried.
+- **Impact:** A temporary network or 429 issue can remove guest badges for the rest of the session, even after connectivity recovers.
+- **FIX:** Only mark IDs as loaded after a successful fetch, or remove failed IDs from the ref and retry them with backoff.
+
+### [P2] Double `Стол` prefix regression in legacy cards
+- **Lines:** 1530, 1635
+- **Problem:** `RequestCard` and `OrderCard` prepend `"Стол "` directly to `tableData.name`. In this codebase, table names are already stored with that prefix, so the UI can render `Стол Стол 5`.
+- **Impact:** Reintroduces a previously fixed display regression and makes table identifiers noisy/confusing for staff.
+- **FIX:** Reuse the guarded pattern already present at 1881-1885 or extract a shared `withTablePrefix()` helper and use it everywhere table names are rendered.
+
+### [P2] Mobile touch targets are undersized in several high-frequency controls
+- **Lines:** 689, 712, 1304, 1558, 2235, 2274, 4231-4251
+- **Problem:** Multiple controls are smaller than the 44px mobile-safe target:
+  - `RequestCard` action button is `h-7` (28px) at 1558
+  - several order/bulk action buttons are `min-h-[36px]`
+  - header icon buttons use `w-9 h-9` (36px)
+- **Impact:** On a restaurant floor, these are easy to mis-tap, especially one-handed or in motion.
+- **FIX:** Raise all interactive controls to at least `44x44`, including icon buttons and small row actions, and expand the favorite-star hit area as well.
+
+### [P2] Production debug logs remain in the page
+- **Lines:** 2980-2987
+- **Problem:** Session cleanup writes to `console.log()` in production.
+- **Impact:** Violates the project rule against debug logs in release code and can leak operational details into production consoles.
+- **FIX:** Remove the logs or route them through a guarded debug logger/telemetry hook that is disabled in production.
+
+## Summary
+- Total findings: 10
+- P0: 0
+- P1: 5
+- P2: 5
+- P3: 0
+
+## Checked And Not Found
+- No `usePartnerAccess()` / `PartnerShell` violation in this file
+- No conditional-hook violation found in the reviewed paths
+- No `dangerouslySetInnerHTML` usage found
+- No `URL.createObjectURL()` / `URL.revokeObjectURL()` usage found

+# Code Review Report: `task-260414-191537` `staffordersmobile.jsx`
+
+Reviewed file:
+- `C:\Dev\worktrees\task-260414-191537\pages\StaffOrdersMobile\staffordersmobile.jsx`
+
+Context reviewed:
+- `C:\Dev\worktrees\task-260414-191537\pages\StaffOrdersMobile\StaffOrdersMobile README.md`
+- `C:\Dev\worktrees\task-260414-191537\pages\StaffOrdersMobile\BUGS.md`
+
+Note:
+- The target worktree is outside the writable sandbox, so this report is saved in the current review repo mirror under `pages/StaffOrdersMobile/`.
+
+## Findings
+
+### [P1] Logout unbind race regressed
+- **Lines:** 3261-3273
+- **Problem:** `handleLogout()` calls `updateLinkMutation.mutate(...)`, then immediately clears local state and redirects after 500ms. If the network request has not completed, the device can remain bound to the token link. `BUGS.md` already lists this as fixed earlier, so the current file has reintroduced the race.
+- **Impact:** Staff can get locked out on the next login because the previous device binding was never reliably cleared.
+- **FIX:** Make `handleLogout` async, await `updateLinkMutation.mutateAsync()` or `base44.entities.StaffAccessLink.update(...)`, handle failure with a toast, then clear local storage and navigate only after the unbind attempt finishes.
+
+### [P1] Order status mutations fail silently and do not surface 429 state
+- **Lines:** 1594-1606, 1904-1920
+- **Problem:** `updateStatusMutation` and `advanceMutation` only roll back optimistic cache in `onError`. They do not show any error toast and do not set `rateLimitHit` on 429 responses, unlike several other mutations in the file.
+- **Impact:** Waiters tap an action, the UI snaps back or does nothing, and there is no explanation. In real service flow this looks like a broken button.
+- **FIX:** In both `onError` handlers, detect `isRateLimitError(err)` and switch into the rate-limit screen path (`cancelQueries()` + `setRateLimitHit(true)`), and show a translated error toast for all non-429 failures.
+
+### [P1] Partner scoping can fall back to global `.list()` queries
+- **Lines:** 3351-3373, 3494-3519
+- **Problem:** `tables`, `orders`, and `serviceRequests` use `.list()` when `partnerId` is falsy:
+  - `Table.list()` at 3371
+  - `Order.list("-created_date", 1000)` at 3496
+  - `ServiceRequest.list()` at 3518
+  Their `enabled` conditions do not consistently require `partnerId`.
+- **Impact:** If link/user data is incomplete or malformed, this page can fetch unscoped cross-restaurant data. In a multi-tenant Base44 app, that is a serious data-isolation bug.
+- **FIX:** Require `!!partnerId` before enabling these queries, remove the global `.list()` fallback, and show a blocking error state when partner context cannot be resolved.
+
+### [P1] i18n is still missing across the page
+- **Lines:** 220-349, 418-420, 921-924, 2914-2930, 3363, 4139-4186, 4217-4552
+- **Problem:** The page uses `useI18n()` only for stage-name translation, but most user-facing UI is still hardcoded in Russian:
+  - `STATUS_FLOW`, `TYPE_THEME`, `REQUEST_TYPE_LABELS`, `HALL_UI_TEXT`, `ROLE_LABELS`
+  - toast messages and dialog labels
+  - header labels and button text
+  - fallbacks like `"Ресторан"`, `"стол"`, `"Ссылка недействительна."`
+  - `formatRelativeTime()` is hard-wired to `date-fns/locale/ru`
+- **Impact:** This violates the project i18n rule and makes the page impossible to localize correctly. `BUGS.md` already tracks this as `BUG-SM-001`, so the issue remains unresolved.
+- **FIX:** Convert text constants into functions that accept `t`, replace all user-facing strings with `t('page.section.key')`, and derive date/number locale from the active i18n locale instead of hardcoding Russian formatting.
+
+### [P1] AudioContext cleanup regression
+- **Lines:** 1038-1065, 2959-2975
+- **Problem:** `createBeep()` allocates an `AudioContext`, and mount logic stores it in `audioRef.current`, but there is no unmount cleanup that calls `ctx.close()`. `BUGS.md` already records this as a previously fixed issue.
+- **Impact:** Re-entering this screen repeatedly can leak audio contexts on mobile browsers, eventually breaking sound notifications or hitting browser context limits.
+- **FIX:** Add a cleanup effect that calls `audioRef.current?.ctx?.close()` on unmount and then clears the ref.
+
+### [P2] Service request and bulk-close failures still have incomplete error feedback
+- **Lines:** 3550-3557, 4167-4178
+- **Problem:** `updateRequestMutation` only handles rate-limit failures; all other errors are silent. `handleCloseAllOrders()` also only handles the rate-limit branch and otherwise exits without any feedback.
+- **Impact:** Staff can tap request actions or bulk-close flows and receive no visible error when the backend rejects the operation.
+- **FIX:** Add translated error toasts for non-429 failures and surface partial batch failures with a summary toast instead of failing silently.
+
+### [P2] Guest-name caching can permanently hide names after transient request failures
+- **Lines:** 3617-3653
+- **Problem:** Guest IDs are inserted into `loadedGuestIdsRef` before loading starts. Each `SessionGuest.get(id)` failure is swallowed with `.catch(() => null)`, so failed IDs remain marked as attempted and are never retried.
+- **Impact:** A temporary network or 429 issue can remove guest badges for the rest of the session, even after connectivity recovers.
+- **FIX:** Only mark IDs as loaded after a successful fetch, or remove failed IDs from the ref and retry them with backoff.
+
+### [P2] Double `Стол` prefix regression in legacy cards
+- **Lines:** 1530, 1635
+- **Problem:** `RequestCard` and `OrderCard` prepend `"Стол "` directly to `tableData.name`. In this codebase, table names are already stored with that prefix, so the UI can render `Стол Стол 5`.
+- **Impact:** Reintroduces a previously fixed display regression and makes table identifiers noisy/confusing for staff.
+- **FIX:** Reuse the guarded pattern already present at 1881-1885 or extract a shared `withTablePrefix()` helper and use it everywhere table names are rendered.
+
+### [P2] Mobile touch targets are undersized in several high-frequency controls
+- **Lines:** 689, 712, 1304, 1558, 2235, 2274, 4231-4251
+- **Problem:** Multiple controls are smaller than the 44px mobile-safe target:
+  - `RequestCard` action button is `h-7` (28px) at 1558
+  - several order/bulk action buttons are `min-h-[36px]`
+  - header icon buttons use `w-9 h-9` (36px)
+- **Impact:** On a restaurant floor, these are easy to mis-tap, especially one-handed or in motion.
+- **FIX:** Raise all interactive controls to at least `44x44`, including icon buttons and small row actions, and expand the favorite-star hit area as well.
+
+### [P2] Production debug logs remain in the page
+- **Lines:** 2980-2987
+- **Problem:** Session cleanup writes to `console.log()` in production.
+- **Impact:** Violates the project rule against debug logs in release code and can leak operational details into production consoles.
+- **FIX:** Remove the logs or route them through a guarded debug logger/telemetry hook that is disabled in production.
+
+## Summary
+- Total findings: 10
+- P0: 0
+- P1: 5
+- P2: 5
+- P3: 0
+
+## Checked And Not Found
+- No `usePartnerAccess()` / `PartnerShell` violation in this file
+- No conditional-hook violation found in the reviewed paths
+- No `dangerouslySetInnerHTML` usage found
+- No `URL.createObjectURL()` / `URL.revokeObjectURL()` usage found

+# Code Review Report: `task-260414-191537` `staffordersmobile.jsx`
+
+Reviewed file:
+- `C:\Dev\worktrees\task-260414-191537\pages\StaffOrdersMobile\staffordersmobile.jsx`
+
+Context reviewed:
+- `C:\Dev\worktrees\task-260414-191537\pages\StaffOrdersMobile\StaffOrdersMobile README.md`
+- `C:\Dev\worktrees\task-260414-191537\pages\StaffOrdersMobile\BUGS.md`
+
+Note:
+- The target worktree is outside the writable sandbox, so this report is saved in the current review repo mirror under `pages/StaffOrdersMobile/`.
+
+## Findings
+
+### [P1] Logout unbind race regressed
+- **Lines:** 3261-3273
+- **Problem:** `handleLogout()` calls `updateLinkMutation.mutate(...)`, then immediately clears local state and redirects after 500ms. If the network request has not completed, the device can remain bound to the token link. `BUGS.md` already lists this as fixed earlier, so the current file has reintroduced the race.
+- **Impact:** Staff can get locked out on the next login because the previous device binding was never reliably cleared.
+- **FIX:** Make `handleLogout` async, await `updateLinkMutation.mutateAsync()` or `base44.entities.StaffAccessLink.update(...)`, handle failure with a toast, then clear local storage and navigate only after the unbind attempt finishes.
+
+### [P1] Order status mutations fail silently and do not surface 429 state
+- **Lines:** 1594-1606, 1904-1920
+- **Problem:** `updateStatusMutation` and `advanceMutation` only roll back optimistic cache in `onError`. They do not show any error toast and do not set `rateLimitHit` on 429 responses, unlike several other mutations in the file.
+- **Impact:** Waiters tap an action, the UI snaps back or does nothing, and there is no explanation. In real service flow this looks like a broken button.
+- **FIX:** In both `onError` handlers, detect `isRateLimitError(err)` and switch into the rate-limit screen path (`cancelQueries()` + `setRateLimitHit(true)`), and show a translated error toast for all non-429 failures.
+
+### [P1] Partner scoping can fall back to global `.list()` queries
+- **Lines:** 3351-3373, 3494-3519
+- **Problem:** `tables`, `orders`, and `serviceRequests` use `.list()` when `partnerId` is falsy:
+  - `Table.list()` at 3371
+  - `Order.list("-created_date", 1000)` at 3496
+  - `ServiceRequest.list()` at 3518
+  Their `enabled` conditions do not consistently require `partnerId`.
+- **Impact:** If link/user data is incomplete or malformed, this page can fetch unscoped cross-restaurant data. In a multi-tenant Base44 app, that is a serious data-isolation bug.
+- **FIX:** Require `!!partnerId` before enabling these queries, remove the global `.list()` fallback, and show a blocking error state when partner context cannot be resolved.
+
+### [P1] i18n is still missing across the page
+- **Lines:** 220-349, 418-420, 921-924, 2914-2930, 3363, 4139-4186, 4217-4552
+- **Problem:** The page uses `useI18n()` only for stage-name translation, but most user-facing UI is still hardcoded in Russian:
+  - `STATUS_FLOW`, `TYPE_THEME`, `REQUEST_TYPE_LABELS`, `HALL_UI_TEXT`, `ROLE_LABELS`
+  - toast messages and dialog labels
+  - header labels and button text
+  - fallbacks like `"Ресторан"`, `"стол"`, `"Ссылка недействительна."`
+  - `formatRelativeTime()` is hard-wired to `date-fns/locale/ru`
+- **Impact:** This violates the project i18n rule and makes the page impossible to localize correctly. `BUGS.md` already tracks this as `BUG-SM-001`, so the issue remains unresolved.
+- **FIX:** Convert text constants into functions that accept `t`, replace all user-facing strings with `t('page.section.key')`, and derive date/number locale from the active i18n locale instead of hardcoding Russian formatting.
+
+### [P1] AudioContext cleanup regression
+- **Lines:** 1038-1065, 2959-2975
+- **Problem:** `createBeep()` allocates an `AudioContext`, and mount logic stores it in `audioRef.current`, but there is no unmount cleanup that calls `ctx.close()`. `BUGS.md` already records this as a previously fixed issue.
+- **Impact:** Re-entering this screen repeatedly can leak audio contexts on mobile browsers, eventually breaking sound notifications or hitting browser context limits.
+- **FIX:** Add a cleanup effect that calls `audioRef.current?.ctx?.close()` on unmount and then clears the ref.
+
+### [P2] Service request and bulk-close failures still have incomplete error feedback
+- **Lines:** 3550-3557, 4167-4178
+- **Problem:** `updateRequestMutation` only handles rate-limit failures; all other errors are silent. `handleCloseAllOrders()` also only handles the rate-limit branch and otherwise exits without any feedback.
+- **Impact:** Staff can tap request actions or bulk-close flows and receive no visible error when the backend rejects the operation.
+- **FIX:** Add translated error toasts for non-429 failures and surface partial batch failures with a summary toast instead of failing silently.
+
+### [P2] Guest-name caching can permanently hide names after transient request failures
+- **Lines:** 3617-3653
+- **Problem:** Guest IDs are inserted into `loadedGuestIdsRef` before loading starts. Each `SessionGuest.get(id)` failure is swallowed with `.catch(() => null)`, so failed IDs remain marked as attempted and are never retried.
+- **Impact:** A temporary network or 429 issue can remove guest badges for the rest of the session, even after connectivity recovers.
+- **FIX:** Only mark IDs as loaded after a successful fetch, or remove failed IDs from the ref and retry them with backoff.
+
+### [P2] Double `Стол` prefix regression in legacy cards
+- **Lines:** 1530, 1635
+- **Problem:** `RequestCard` and `OrderCard` prepend `"Стол "` directly to `tableData.name`. In this codebase, table names are already stored with that prefix, so the UI can render `Стол Стол 5`.
+- **Impact:** Reintroduces a previously fixed display regression and makes table identifiers noisy/confusing for staff.
+- **FIX:** Reuse the guarded pattern already present at 1881-1885 or extract a shared `withTablePrefix()` helper and use it everywhere table names are rendered.
+
+### [P2] Mobile touch targets are undersized in several high-frequency controls
+- **Lines:** 689, 712, 1304, 1558, 2235, 2274, 4231-4251
+- **Problem:** Multiple controls are smaller than the 44px mobile-safe target:
+  - `RequestCard` action button is `h-7` (28px) at 1558
+  - several order/bulk action buttons are `min-h-[36px]`
+  - header icon buttons use `w-9 h-9` (36px)
+- **Impact:** On a restaurant floor, these are easy to mis-tap, especially one-handed or in motion.
+- **FIX:** Raise all interactive controls to at least `44x44`, including icon buttons and small row actions, and expand the favorite-star hit area as well.
+
+### [P2] Production debug logs remain in the page
+- **Lines:** 2980-2987
+- **Problem:** Session cleanup writes to `console.log()` in production.
+- **Impact:** Violates the project rule against debug logs in release code and can leak operational details into production consoles.
+- **FIX:** Remove the logs or route them through a guarded debug logger/telemetry hook that is disabled in production.
+
+## Summary
+- Total findings: 10
+- P0: 0
+- P1: 5
+- P2: 5
+- P3: 0
+
+## Checked And Not Found
+- No `usePartnerAccess()` / `PartnerShell` violation in this file
+- No conditional-hook violation found in the reviewed paths
+- No `dangerouslySetInnerHTML` usage found
+- No `URL.createObjectURL()` / `URL.revokeObjectURL()` usage found
